04/06/2019, 09:36 - Kate: *KICK DECIET OUT OF YOUR LIPS IF YOU MUST LIVE A LIFE OF INTEGRITY*

Deceit is one sure way of identifying a person who lacks integrity. A person of integrity will stand for truth and will speak the truth no matter what it might cost them.

Today, when it comes to sin, we categorize it on a weighing scale. We make alarm for some while we take others as a usual thing done daily. However, we must understand that God looks at all sins as sin. None is sin above the other. When someone commits adultery or murder, and another tells lies, they have all committed sin and in the eyes of God, none is a small sinner. 

We have been raised in societies that lack spiritual morals where lying is the order of the day. Husbands lie to wives, and so do wives to keep their marriage going. Shepherds lie to the sheep and so does the sheep.  Parents lie to their children and so do children, teachers lie to students and so do students. Employers lie to their employees to keep the company going.  Leaders lie to their followers, to be submissive to them. Itâ€™s a vicious circle of deceit.

Sometimes we use lies as a means of getting what we what and then excuse ourselves of hardships in the economy, political issues, that is how I would get to where I wanted. It is the only way I would protect my marriage. It was easier to lie so I would have him propose to me. I needed a job to fend for my children and had no option but to lie. I needed a visa to travel to USA.

Many people have accumulated a lot of wealth through deceit. Others have got into marriages because at one point they had to lie. Others have got citizenship of other countries only because they had to fake some stories to go through it. Women are forging sickness on their children because that is the only way a man would give her money. Others are escaping to pay taxes by forging documents. Many are calling themselves widows, orphans because by so doing, they can win sympathy of sponsors. Etc!

This is the bitter shock behind many peoples success; But we must not forget that God hates lying. Proverbs 6 verses 16-19 lists seven things God hates, and itâ€™s worth noting that two of them refer to dishonesty: _*â€œThere are six things the Lord hates no, seven things he detests: haughty eyes, a lying tongue, hands that kill the innocent, a heart that plots evil, feet that race to do wrong, a false witness who pours out lies, a person who sows discord in a family.â€_*

Therefore God cannot stand with us to protect whatever we got through deceit. The Bible says in Isaiah 54:14 _*â€˜â€™In righteousness you will be established: Tyranny will be far from you; you will have nothing to fear. Terror will be far removed; it will not come near you.â€™â€™*_ So if we use a crooked way to succeed,  the end might not be that good.

Because the Devil is the originator of deception there is no single lie that we will speak that will not be found. Shockingly, we might even be dead already, but it will catch up with our children. Why? Because lies are for the devil and the same devil who inspires us to lie, will use the same route to expose us.

In John 8:44, Jesus says the following of the devil, "He was a murderer from the beginning, and does not stand in the truth, because there is no truth in him. When he lies, he speaks out of his own character, for he is a liar and the father of lies." Not only does the devil deceive, He is the father of deception.

If we must live a life of INTEGRITY, let us speak nothing but the truth all the time. It does not matter where truth will take us but speaking it will save us from a lot of troubles and shame. Not forgetting to remind ourselves that speaking the truth and knowing the truth shall always set us free from the chains of the enemy. We are not in this world to impress people, if we must get something through deceit, it is much better not to get it.

By the grace of God, speaking the truth is very possible through Jesus Christ, and so we are able to aim towards true integrity for ourselves.

"Whoever walks in integrity walks securely, but he who makes his ways crooked will be found out." Proverbs 10:9

22.After reading a good message, try to say" Thanks for the message". APPRECIATION remains the easiest way of getting what you don't have.
Rev Titus

*THE DANGER OF CARELESS WORDS!* 

Careless words have destroyed more relationships than any other human vice. The tongue is a knife that can cut another person deeper than any sword. So the next time you're tempted to make a comment at someone else's expense, take just a moment to think before you speak. You may be glad you did.

 Some of us blindly say that as long as what weâ€™re saying is the truth, itâ€™s Ok. But honesty that does not have the best interest of the other person at heart is really a cruel form of selfishness. How do you tell your spouse how you hate fat bellies well knowing that theirs isn't small? 

*JESUS SAID:* 

*_â€œYou can be sure that on the Judgment Day you will have to give account of every useless word you have ever spoken. ~Matthew 12:36GNT_*

 *THEREFORE:* 

*_Let your speech at all times be gracious and pleasant, seasoned with salt, so that you will know how to answer each one [who questions you]. Think Before You Speak. ~Colossians 4:6AMP_*

 *NEVER FORGET:*

 _There are moments in life, when the heart is so full of emotion That if by chance it be shaken, or into its depths like a pebble Drops some careless word, it overflows, and its secret, Spilt on the ground like water, can never be gathered together. ~Henry Wadsworth Longfellow_

02/07/2019, 05:12 - Aunt Dora: POLICE DOGS RECOGNIZE CHRIST IN THE EUCHARIST...

"On the evening of the last day of his October 1995 visit to the United States, John Paul II was scheduled to greet the seminarians at Saint Maryâ€™s Seminary in Baltimore. It had been a very full day that began with a Mass at Oriole Park in Camden Yards, a parade through downtown streets, a visit to the Basilica of the Assumption, the first cathedral in the country, lunch at a local soup kitchen run by Catholic Charities; a prayer service at the Cathedral of Mary Our Queen in North Baltimore; and finally a quick stop at Saint Maryâ€™s Seminary.

The schedule was tight so the plan was simply to greet the seminarians while they stood outside on the steps. But the Pope made his way through their ranks and into the building. His plan was to first make a visit to the Blessed Sacrament.

When his wishes were made known, security flew into action. They swept the building paying close attention to the chapel where the Pope would be praying. For this purpose highly trained dogs were used to detect any person who might be present.

The dogs are trained to locate survivors in collapsed buildings after earthquakes and other disasters. These highly intelligent and eager dogs quickly went through the halls, offices and classrooms and were then sent to the chapel. They went up and down the aisle, past the pews and finally into the side chapel where the Blessed Sacrament is reserved.

Upon reaching the tabernacle, the dogs sniffed, whined, pointed, and refused to leave, their attention riveted on the tabernacle, until called by their handlers. They were convinced that they discovered someone there.

We Catholics know they were right â€” they found a real, living Person in the tabernacle!!!"

by Domenico Bettinelli.

24/07/2019, 16:13 - John Thomas: A Kampala high court was on Friday thrown into uncontrollable laughter and shouts  in a divorce matter. 
The respondent, a middle aged man  wasn't represented by counsel. He was humble and looked pitiable. 

When asked if he was contesting the divorce, his answer was touching. He said if that is what will bring happiness to the petitioner, he wasn't contesting. 

Next,  were the petitioner's demands for custody of the 3 children and maintenance fee  monthly. Again, the respondent conceeded cheerfully. 

Then the thunderbolt! The respondent made his solatry request. The court was dead quiet. 

Respondent requested for custody of the 22 year busty housemaid. For certainty and unambiguty he pointed at her in court. She stood up for recognition. 

The petitioner went wild in protest. She ignored her counsel and shouted no! no! no!  no way. 

When calm returned, the judge asked the respondent why he wanted custody of the beautiful busty housemaid. 

The respondent replied that he conceeded to all demands of the petitioner to make her happy. Now he's requesting for only one thing to make him happy, yet petitioner has gone wild. 

My Lord, you can see for yourself what I have been going through for the past 27 years of the marriage! Petitioner wants only her happiness, mine not included.. That has been my silent burden. 

The petitioner then charged at the maid and the respondent which drew laughter from the audience. The court was forced into recess to talk to the parties in chamber.

What should My Lord do in your esteemed opinion???

09/08/2019, 22:52 - Aunt Dora: *WHAT IS THE BLESSED SACRAMENTâ—â—â—*
An exorcist priest from Canada gave a talk in which he explained * the importance of adoring the Blessed Sacrament * for at least one hour a week.
And for people who suffer from strong illnesses or have problems with some of their family members, he said that going to worship for half an hour or an hour a day, not only cure; but it transforms everything. It is the maximum. The priest also gave some guidelines on how to do the adoration ...
*Example:*
* The first 15 minutes * go before Jesus in the Eucharist, and tell Him that you love Him and that you want to allow yourself  to be loved by Him.
* The next 15 minutes * Thank Him for everything:
For life
For family
For what we have to eat
For work or business
For the water we have to bathe. Etc...
Many, he said, no longer give thanks because we do not value what we have, but we always look at what we do not have.
* After do 15 min of reparation *
Repairing and delivering of our relatives who do not know Him do not love Him ...
Reparation for the terrible things that are happening in the world: Abortions, idolatries, massacres, adulteries, etc ...
*And use the last 15 minutes to make  requests*
He mentioned that he gave the 15 minute times as a guide, but it does not necessarily have to be those times.
He also said that whoever has a disease like cancer, if he goes to the Blessed Sacrament to do adoration, does not lose weight, does not lose his hair, or feel strong pain. He said that from an exposed Blessed Sacrament Jesus' rays are coming out and people get healed and delivered.
* If you want, you can Share this * ... So that everyone knows the importance of Adoration to the Most Blessed Sacrament *

24/08/2019, 19:03 - Aunt Dora: Where did Bad Black go? Where did SK Mbuga go? Where did Mike Ezra go? Where did Amama Mbabazi go? I have not lived for a very long time, but I have seen things change.

I have seen men who would 'kujooga' this country sink into oblivion. Maybe it is really true, we all just have our 15 minutes of fame and they soon pass.

When I had just joined Facebook, the celebs of those days were Henry Jr Maks, Divine Marley, General Sweetman. Today no one even remembers them.

Who did not witness the days when WBS TV was the thing? We even had an anthem; 'WBS eyange...tv station esinga...abiiri mutaano ku TV ğŸ“º yo...WBS etusse." People where is WBS now?

What happened to Barbara Yata? Do you people even remember that name? What about PAM Awards? Ragga Dee even sang a song displaying all his awards.

It is funny, we just see these things and never learn from them. Doreen Kabareebe was the talk of the town. Today, hardly anyone can recognize her if she walked by. 

Just because you are having your 15 minutes of fame should not get to your head. Your minutes too shall pass.

I have seen girls that every man yearned for become girls that no man notices. I have seen men who had nothing become something. Life keeps changing its house. Today it may be in your house, it may leave tomorrow.

Just because you have made some little money, and invested in your rentals should not make you think you have arrived. I have seen men sell off everything they had and return to zero. Today's gold is tomorrow's copper.

Do you remember when the mobile phone had just become popular in this country? What happened? 

Lesson in all this, just be humble. Don't let success get to your head and don't look down on anyone who is not having it yet well.

If you have a job, reach out and try to get your friends into jobs. Who knows? If you have money, take off some of it and help a friend or relative. Karma is a real bitch. 

Today you may be on top, tomorrow you could be totally nothing. One of the books that changed my life were Nassim Taleb's Black Swan and Fooled by Randomness.

Life is very random. Yet people keep thinking it is all about their might, their intelligence. How foolish of them!!! Today you are walking all healthy, tomorrow you can wake up to a terminal illness diagnosis. And that will instantly alter your life. Life can change in split seconds. I have seen destinies change in seconds. All of a sudden, the key person of a family, club, group or organization dies and itâ€™s  back to zero, back to eating crumbs, no ideas or principlesğŸ¤·ğŸ¿â€â™€ğŸ¤·ğŸ¿â€â™€

That's why I laugh at people when they get some fame, some little money and become stupidly arrogant. Many more like you have come, many more like you have have gone.

Those of us who were on Myspace remember the celebs of Myspace. Now where is Myspace today? Where is Yahoo? 

I can go on and on. Too many examples. So when you get your 15 minutes of fame, use them wisely. And always remember, what goes around comes around. Even Fooda was a hit song....

The Baganda say; 'N'ebiibimba bbika.." 
Don't despise anyone.
Be humble.

30/08/2019, 18:38 - Joanna: *Moving out of the Comfort Zone*

Once there was a king who received a gift of two magnificent falcons. They were peregrine falcons, the most beautiful birds he had ever seen. He gave the precious birds to his head falconer to be trained.

Months passed, and one day the head falconer informed the king that though one of the falcons was flying majestically, soaring high in the sky, the other bird had not moved from its branch since the day it had arrived.

The king summoned healers and sorcerers from all the land to tend to the falcon, but no one could make the bird fly.

He presented the task to the member of his court, but the next day, the king saw through the palace window that the bird had still not moved from its perch.

Having tried everything else, the king thought to himself, â€œMay be I need someone more familiar with the countryside to understand the nature of this problem.â€ So he cried out to his court, â€œGo and get a farmer.â€

In the morning, the king was thrilled to see the falcon soaring high above the palace gardens. He said to his court, â€œBring me the doer of this miracle.â€

The court quickly located the farmer, who came and stood before the king. The king asked him, â€œHow did you make the falcon fly?â€

With his head bowed, the farmer said to the king, â€œIt was very easy, your highness. I simply cut the branch where the bird was sitting.â€

LESSON:
We are all made to fly â€” to realize our incredible potential as human beings. But at times we sit on our branches, clinging to the things that are familiar to us. 
The possibilities are endless, but for most of us, they remain undiscovered. We conform to the familiar, the comfortable, and the mundane. So for the most part, our lives are mediocre instead of exciting, thrilling and fulfilling. Let us learn to destroy the branch of fear we cling to and free ourselves to the glory of flight!

What you will need for the case of severe ulcers and tumors 
- raw pawpaw - 1 medium size
- aloe vera  gel- 2 tablespoons 
- black seeds- 1 teaspoon 
- soursop- 1 teaspoon 
- Bermuda grass powder - 1 teaspoon ( also good for PCOs, UTIs and STIs) 
-dandelion - 1 teaspoon 

How to prepare 
Get a medium size raw papaya wash it very well and slice off it's bottom to reveal  a hole-like inside. 

Then staff the raw pawpaw with all or some of the above mentioned herbs. 

Add hot water into the pawpaw 

Now cover the staffed paw paw and allow the content to brew over night. 

Strain the content and keep in an air tight container. 

Then take 1/4 glass of the content  3 times a day at least 30 minutes before meals.

Do this for 1 month to have the ulcers disappear. 

You may add honey to improve  taste. 

Best of luck to all who wish to try. 

Let food be thy medicine.

Yesterday i got home past midnight very late after a certain function in NamasubağŸ˜¥. And because i did not have any other means of transport i decided to use a boda boda despite being warned by my friend not to.

I insisted and boarded this boda boda. On my way home i started getting suspicious and scared at how this boda boda guy was staring at me strangely through his side mirror.

We finally reached my destination at Bunamwaya and got off the boda boda, i reached for my pass and handed 10k to him and asked him to keep the change as well so that he could atleast spare my life.

I then immediately turned to walk away to my house and this is where my #Nightmare begun. The guy started following me. I moved faster and the guy got the speed too .....

I knew this was trouble so i started running to the opposite direction and he chased me. At that time i felt so helpless because i knew no one would come to my rescue since it was so late in the night.

I got so tired at a certain point and decided to face this guy. He grabbed my hand and he softly said this to me, "Please give me my #helmet",  its at that time that i realised i was still wearing his helmet. 

Am now seated in my sitting room watching a movie. Good day!

 -Sunday - *Wangu*
-Monday - *Kazooba*
-Tuesday - *Walumbe*

-Thursday - *Kiwanuka*
-Friday - *Nagawooye*
-Saturday - *Wamunyi*

 -January - *Gatoonya*
-February - *Mukutulansanja*
-March - *Mugulansingo*
-April - *Kafumulampawu*
-May - *Muzigo*
-June - *Ssebo aseka*

-August - *Muwakanya*
-September - *Mutunda*

12/11/2019, 23:43 - Aunt Dora: MY LIFE LESSONS  BY . HON.ODONGA OTTO MP UGANDA 
Thanks for all birthday wishes.I  was told by my late father James otto that i was born on 11th November 1977 a date i doubt firstly  because my mum was killed by karimojong cattle rustlers in 1987 she could have known the dates better,secondly my elder brother David also told me that my father told him  the same date as his birthday.it doesn't matter, years move in a linear manner it doesnt move in a  round manner for a birthday to repeat it self,its just human codification for ease of reference in passports, documents etc but please read my story###longpost warning:####
My chilhood was the most difficult that i think no one reading this post has  ever gine through a similar experience those who knew me from under fiteen years can testify.
My father separated with my mother at the time i was born that is why my mother called me :"odonga" meaning let him remain with me.
Secondly my father made a decision i term the worst to take me with him to my step mother  at the time of divorce.

LESSON 1:mothers die with your child dont ever allow your child to grow up with step mother the world would rather end.

My Dad got arrested by the UPC goverment in 1980/1 and spent 5 years in luzira prison.I was left with a step mother who  is still alive.My late  mother did not know my  whereabouts  and even if she did she probably had no authority over my custody.
During those 5 years of dad being in prison i visited hell on earth,My eldest brother Tadeo went to boarding school negri primary my second bother david was "deported" to the village and he is a P.7 dropout

LESSON 2 :see what education  has done it has  now created two seperate  biengs from the same womb  give education your best it replaces an empty head 

I remained alone to a young step mother about 27 years  she was a teacher .I would be locked in a room from morning to evening as there was no one to look after me,with one meal for the day kept in the room. 
Barely 5 years occasionally i would climb through the vents to see my friends playing in the compound the feeling still sends a chill down my spine.
Needless to say the room (prison) was not self contained  she would return to get the room in a mess and a stick would do the cleaning.
Years I later on 1984 i  joined P.1 in negri primary,i was about 7 years that was the first and last memorable time in my life i saw my late  mother. she took advantage of the visitation to visit her son whi she had not seen  in years who now in a boarding school from."prison".She was tall in brown outfit it was called "maxi" then. she lifted me high and i gave her a long list of things to bring on the next visition ,little did i know it was the last time i was seeing her .

LESSON 3 :readers in life when hugging a dear one please bear in mind it may be the last time ,give it your best .

uncle paul years later came and told my mother was dead i was not bothered because i had not bonded with her i continued playing, she died of bullet wounds.
 
My formative years from P.4 to S.4 was the worst superintended by my step mother, extreme use of mannual labour as a means of tourture in the name of hard work ;each one head a drum of water to fill before going to school,our mornings would begin at 5am by 7 am each ones 200liters drum is to be full daily before going to school and  the body is too tired for school.

Digging weekends 7am to 7pm at stepmothers home was routine   we would do close to what a tractor could do in day.Passers by in the morning would wonder in the evening how 3 peoples(brothers could do this).
Rationing food,stravation ,washing plates ,pounding,washing house walls,washing her clothes and those of all her sisters who had migrated permanently to our home, was on the daily menu.As they sat a watched movies.

LESSON 4, Dont let visitors at your home turn your own children into slaves.

My luck came when i got a vocation to join a seminary that had no option of day schooling,my brothers where not allowed in boardong school .And that finally made a difference in our eventual academic performance.
I remember my stepmother calling my elder brother at 8am to slash the compound yet that was the day he was sitting for national UCE examinations,he had already  fetched his morning  rountine 200litre  drum of water,i had to join him to slash the compound non stop for upto 15  minutes to exam time then he had to run 8kms to school to catch up with exam time.He was late and didnt do we...he later told he just wrote his name and sat since it was chemistry he hated.

LESSON 5 ,don't use work as a punishement or a torture tool.

I  completed O,level,A lelvel joined Univesity and came out with a degree in social sciences .my graduation was not attended by any of my parents,i walked to freedom square typical.of lumumba hall courage and got my degree there was not voice to ululate for me as the read my name ,i stood behind with no peny in my pocket, and a kind old man Mr. Odida Francis got me a gown  took for lunch at tick hotel kawempe.I enjoyed the chips and chicken .Now the whole world was ahead of me.  I later took my degree home to my father and stepmother.My stepmother who also had 5  children  was never happy for me having attained a degree.My degree created more unease home as i waited for a job.I was later told by my stepmother that i was to help in home chores of collect residues of food from a girls  secondary  school Sacred heart to feed the pigs ,secondly that I was to cut grass to feed the friesian cows.
Beacuse i did not want to disapoint my Dad who had already leactured me on Pope John paul II missive towards work ,i opted to secretly get a teaching job at atiak technical that was displaced in gulu town ,to teach English and use the proceeds to hire young boys to do the dirty job of delivering the pig food.Word reached home of my evasive and nagative attitude to work and there was a bigger conference than the 1884 berlin conference or the 1914 Versailles peace traeaty  that i had just studied at university called at home .It was resolved i stop teaching and concentrate on feeding the animals 
I continied teaching secretly.

LESSON 6 men when you are in a second marriage or polygamous marriage beware  and warn yourself that love for the children may follow the  love for their mother,for the woman you love most  you will tend to  love her children more  "mutatus mutandi "..BEWARE.

I later started doing the job of collecting pig food,at wee hours cutting grass for  cows in distant locations.This did not help.In life  some people can never change and can't be amused of their objective is harm another meeting was called over this new developements of me cutting graas from far and  rules changed and they started designating places that i should cut grass.
That the issue was to deal with  was pride of having a degree and not mere cutting grass or collecting pig food.For me i was obtaining the desired results others where looking at the means.
The next morning my step mother told me there was good grass at the current acholi inn hotel and i was told to go and cut grass there, mind you this was a  ground where few graduates  sat and analysed global trends,the pressure was building on me.Secondly that the food at lunch time at girls schools was more so she had  talked to a staff that i should be there at 12noon and pick food as girls dropped  since there was competition for the same food by others.
Her children where much younger and in primary and secondary school and would have been the best for such jobs in my opinion.my options where getting limited.
I remembered Dr.Simba in a political science class wondering ; what would the importance of education be to those at home if graduates are not seen as role models.
I gathered courage and told my step mother two things one,please let your children do it,secondly even if the pigs food would make the pigs grow like a ballon being blown I AM NOT GOING

LESSON 7 when life seem empty when you feel there is no point going push a little if nothing changes you have to make a decision.

My stepmother broke down in tears shouting that i had abused i hurried to the house before my Dad could drop home for lunch break that would be bad i knew if he found me home.
I packed my things in a kavera polythine bag off through the backyard going to "i dont know where".
I reach town boarded a vehicle to my mothes  clan home,where i was received and felt soo loved for the first tiime in years

LESSON 8:there are times in life you have to learn to make fast decisions, a bad decsion is better than no decision at all.

I later went to the village to visit my cousins and maternal relatives the first time in 22 years of my life what a feeling of joy  and welcome .I broke down in tears to know there where people who loved and cared for me,i met my late  mothers  sister and uncles i had to become a baby and cry abit.I saw my younger sister struggling preparing sorghurm posho for lunch with smoke belowing in the entire grass tatch house i could hardly breath.I ate lunch and asked for a hoe to go digging i knew i had in built capacity to work.She  looked at me in the eyes and said "its dry season"

LESSON 9 :In life no mater the spite ,riducle,hatred,abuses,agrresion towards you,jealousy etc just know you are loved by someone,there are people who love you ,who dont sleep thinking of you so please love yourself don't give up .

I later saw a vacuum being the only graduate in the village i contested for parliamentary elections 6 months after university and deafeated the incumbent  minister of education Hon. Alfred Ogaba and become elected member of parliament aruu county pader district in the year 2000 at 23 years making the record then  of being  the youngest Member of parliament  in uganda.i have never worked any where since in this is my fisrt job.

Todate i have been an MP for 18 years thank God,i have 6 children(4   girls 2 boys) , my first marriage failed . I obtaies a master degree and a another Degree in law i am now an advocate. I live in a comfortable house of my own ,drive and a few businesses, i now employ abot 30 ugandans on full time basis.while In parliament given my childhood memories I choose to speak for the oppressed and would prefer that i be  the last on the list of oppression.I   am very sensitive to my children issues  when  my two older daughters  come to stay with me i keep a watchfull eye.
MEN don't be in bars come home late and think your wife is good to be with her step children hey...she is probably worse than mine.

LESSON 10: Keep your faith ,when there is no room for rationality or reasoning follow your instincts whatever route you take  your God will always be with you.
whichever route you take you will see light at the end of the turnel endure,.. endure ...endure.your sufferings should not be in vain.

42 years down the road,my two elelder brothers just like me  are grappling with life arising from a detented childhood Just like  the prisoners during the french revolution when the bastile prison was broken 11 inmates found in  three  weeks later  went back on their own volition  even when the prison doors where wide  open.They had overstayed in prison and gotten used.we overstayed in oppression.my father died 4 years ago,my stepmother has since become a "catechist"after my fathers death,a catechist with a locked borehole home not accessible to neighbours.Of my 5 step brothers who had  preferential treatment in early chilhood  2 are drivers,one a lawyer,one a chef and one remains unemployed.I reburied my mother 10 years ago.
My story is like of Joseph in Egypt,i rose from grass to grace thank.God.
LESSON 11: The stone the builders have rejected has become the corner house stone,don't mistreat peoples children it will bring misfortunes to yours.
PLEASE SHARE THIS POST I MAY BE A CELEBRITY IN MANY EYES IN UGANDA BUT YOU DONT KNOW WHAT I WENT THROUGH,.... .PEOPLE DONT KNOW WHAT YOU ARE GOING THROUGH.... PEOPLE DONT KNOW WHAT YOUR CHILDREN ARE GOING THROUGH.....PEOPLE DONT KNOW WHAT  OTHER CHILDREN ARE GOING THROUGH.
THANKS FOR THE BIRTHDAY WISHES
PLEASE SHARE.....if there are those who think they have problems let then see my story and learn  that success doesnt come easy
